# Speakeasy Prompt Rewrite (First-Principles v1)

From-scratch rewrite focused on: identity lock, wardrobe fidelity, micro-physics realism, and strict non-explicit compliance.

## Prompt 02 - Piano Edge Potential

### Primary Prompt

MISSION:
Create a premium non-explicit nightlife editorial frame with exact identity fidelity, strong physics realism, and consistent microdetail.

GOAL ORDER (HARD):
1) Identity fidelity + direct lens eye contact.
2) Wardrobe fidelity: exact garment topology, colors, seam map, and material behavior.
3) Pose mechanics: human-plausible balance, support loads, and coherent contact points.
4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- piano edge potential with intentional nightlife atmosphere and strong physical plausibility.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- Grand piano with visible keys, velvet drape, candle sconces, polished wood floor.

WARDROBE LOCK (EXACT):
- Preserve exact wardrobe topology, color mapping, seams, and material behavior from reference intent.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- Balanced full-body stance with direct eye contact, active hands, and clear load path.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- Support reaction -> pelvic orientation -> ribcage counter-rotation -> limb tension -> grounded foot mechanics.

CAMERA + LIGHTING PROFILE:
- Full-frame mirrorless profile; close editorial distance; practical key + controlled rim; realistic depth of field.

COMPOSITION REQUIREMENTS:
- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.


### Safe Backup Prompt

MISSION:
Create a stability-safe backup frame preserving the same identity, wardrobe, pose intent, and physics realism with strict non-explicit compliance.

MANDATORY LOCKS:
- Exact identity and direct eye contact.
- Exact wardrobe topology/colors/material behavior.
- Exact pose intent and support mechanics.
- Non-explicit framing and adult-only presentation.

SCENE PRESERVATION:
- Grand piano with visible keys, velvet drape, candle sconces, polished wood floor.

WARDROBE PRESERVATION:
- Exact wardrobe topology, colors, seam map, and material behavior from primary intent.

POSE + KINEMATIC PRESERVATION:
- Balanced full-body pose with direct gaze and coherent support mechanics.
- Support reaction -> pelvic orientation -> ribcage counter-rotation -> limb tension -> grounded foot mechanics.

SAFE PHYSICS CHECKS (ALL PASS):
- Inverse-square light falloff and coherent practical-light gradients.
- Contact compression + contact shadows at heels/seat/hand interfaces.
- Human-plausible center-of-mass support and joint ranges.
- Wrinkle hierarchy and seam-tension continuity under pose load.
- Reflection/contact integrity with no detached artifacts.
- Natural sensor grain and realistic depth transition.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe drift, geometry fusion.
- Plastic skin, detached shadows/reflections, impossible balance.
- Conservative restyle or explicit framing.


---

### Primary Prompt

2) Wardrobe fidelity: exact garment topology, colors, seam map, and material behavior.
3) Pose mechanics: human-plausible balance, support loads, and coherent contact points.
4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- neon booth refraction with intentional nightlife atmosphere and strong physical plausibility.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- Booth seating, rain-streaked window, neon OPEN glow, candle votives.

WARDROBE LOCK (EXACT):
- Preserve exact wardrobe topology, color mapping, seams, and material behavior from reference intent.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- Balanced full-body stance with direct eye contact, active hands, and clear load path.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- Support reaction -> pelvic orientation -> ribcage counter-rotation -> limb tension -> grounded foot mechanics.

CAMERA + LIGHTING PROFILE:
- Full-frame mirrorless profile; close editorial distance; practical key + controlled rim; realistic depth of field.

COMPOSITION REQUIREMENTS:
- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.

5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

- casino cage mutiny with intentional nightlife atmosphere and strong physical plausibility.

- mirrored column fragments
- amber sconces
- low cigar haze

4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- speakeasy wireline with intentional nightlife atmosphere and strong physical plausibility.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- catwalk grating
- hanging Edison bulbs
- brass handrail
- dark lounge depth

WARDROBE LOCK (EXACT):
- Preserve exact wardrobe topology, color mapping, seams, and material behavior from reference intent.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- Balanced full-body stance with direct eye contact, active hands, and clear load path.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- Support reaction -> pelvic orientation -> ribcage counter-rotation -> limb tension -> grounded foot mechanics.

CAMERA + LIGHTING PROFILE:
- Full-frame mirrorless profile; close editorial distance; practical key + controlled rim; realistic depth of field.

COMPOSITION REQUIREMENTS:
- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.

4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- private velvet booth chamber at last call with intimate tension.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- deep burgundy banquette, brass lamp pool, coupe reflections, low smoke veil.
- intimate environment lock: private-hour nightlife mood, low-key practicals with warm/cool contrast, no sterile daytime or generic lobby atmosphere.

WARDROBE LOCK (EXACT):
- obsidian liquid-satin micro-corset bandeau with sheer side channels + midnight-garnet high-slit bias skirt with contour seam, jet-black thigh-high stockings, lacquered stilettos.
- Styling edge lock: preserve assertive cut lines and fabric tension (slit/mesh/cutout intent); never conservative-restyle or merge into one-piece topology.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- booth-edge perch with lead thigh projection, trailing leg elongated, one hand on booth back, chin angled down with direct gaze.
- close-range pose lock: one weight-bearing leg plus one display leg, visible S-curve through ankle-hip-sternum, active fingers/jawline/core tension, direct-lens intimacy without explicit content.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- seat-edge load -> pelvic cant -> ribcage counter-rotation -> slit flare line -> calf tension -> heel-ground lock.
- Anatomy guardrail: human-plausible joint ranges only; clear load path from support to pelvis to ribcage to gaze; no hyperextension or disconnected limb angles.

CAMERA + LIGHTING PROFILE:
- Canon R5 II, 45mm, f/1.8, 1/200s, ISO 1250, warm practical key + cool rim spill.

COMPOSITION REQUIREMENTS:
- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.

Create a premium non-explicit nightlife editorial frame with exact identity fidelity, strong physics realism, and consistent microdetail.

GOAL ORDER (HARD):
1) Identity fidelity + direct lens eye contact.
2) Wardrobe fidelity: exact garment topology, colors, seam map, and material behavior.
3) Pose mechanics: human-plausible balance, support loads, and coherent contact points.
4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- penthouse fireplace lounge portrait with close cinematic tension.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- stone hearth glow, velvet chaise, skyline bokeh, fine haze ribbon.
- intimate environment lock: private-hour nightlife mood, low-key practicals with warm/cool contrast, no sterile daytime or generic lobby atmosphere.

WARDROBE LOCK (EXACT):
- molten-copper plunge contour crop with chain trim + charcoal high-break slit skirt with bias drape, black thigh-high stockings, bronze stilettos.
- Styling edge lock: preserve assertive cut lines and fabric tension (slit/mesh/cutout intent); never conservative-restyle or merge into one-piece topology.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- chaise-side split stance with one arm trailing along hearth ledge, sternum opened toward camera.
- close-range pose lock: one weight-bearing leg plus one display leg, visible S-curve through ankle-hip-sternum, active fingers/jawline/core tension, direct-lens intimacy without explicit content.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- ledge support -> shoulder extension -> ribcage yaw -> pelvic tilt -> slit opening vector -> forefoot stabilization.
- Anatomy guardrail: human-plausible joint ranges only; clear load path from support to pelvis to ribcage to gaze; no hyperextension or disconnected limb angles.

CAMERA + LIGHTING PROFILE:
- Sony A7R V, 45mm, f/2.0, 1/160s, ISO 1200, fire practical + city rim.

COMPOSITION REQUIREMENTS:
- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.


### Safe Backup Prompt

MISSION:
Create a stability-safe backup frame preserving the same identity, wardrobe, pose intent, and physics realism with strict non-explicit compliance.

MANDATORY LOCKS:
- Exact identity and direct eye contact.
- Exact wardrobe topology/colors/material behavior.
- Exact pose intent and support mechanics.
- Non-explicit framing and adult-only presentation.

SCENE PRESERVATION:
- stone hearth glow, velvet chaise, skyline bokeh, fine haze ribbon.
- intimate environment lock: private-hour nightlife mood, low-key practicals with warm/cool contrast, no sterile daytime or generic lobby atmosphere.

- molten-copper plunge contour crop with chain trim + charcoal high-break slit skirt with bias drape, black thigh-high stockings, bronze stilettos.

POSE + KINEMATIC PRESERVATION:
- chaise-side split stance with one arm trailing along hearth ledge, sternum opened toward camera.
- close-range pose lock: one weight-bearing leg plus one display leg, visible S-curve through ankle-hip-sternum, active fingers/jawline/core tension, direct-lens intimacy without explicit content.
- ledge support -> shoulder extension -> ribcage yaw -> pelvic tilt -> slit opening vector -> forefoot stabilization.
- Anatomy guardrail: human-plausible joint ranges only; clear load path from support to pelvis to ribcage to gaze; no hyperextension or disconnected limb angles.

SAFE PHYSICS CHECKS (ALL PASS):
- Inverse-square light falloff and coherent practical-light gradients.
- Contact compression + contact shadows at heels/seat/hand interfaces.
- Human-plausible center-of-mass support and joint ranges.
- Wrinkle hierarchy and seam-tension continuity under pose load.
- Reflection/contact integrity with no detached artifacts.
- Natural sensor grain and realistic depth transition.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe drift, geometry fusion.
- Plastic skin, detached shadows/reflections, impossible balance.
- Conservative restyle or explicit framing.

1) Identity fidelity + direct lens eye contact.
2) Wardrobe fidelity: exact garment topology, colors, seam map, and material behavior.
3) Pose mechanics: human-plausible balance, support loads, and coherent contact points.
4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- private art-vault lounge portrait with controlled intimate energy.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- charcoal gallery walls, candle tables, sculpture edge silhouette, haze depth.
- intimate environment lock: private-hour nightlife mood, low-key practicals with warm/cool contrast, no sterile daytime or generic lobby atmosphere.

WARDROBE LOCK (EXACT):
- blood-orange contour corset crop with narrow mesh bridge + cobalt high-slit sculpted skirt with side cinch seam, black thigh-high stockings, pointed heels.
- Styling edge lock: preserve assertive cut lines and fabric tension (slit/mesh/cutout intent); never conservative-restyle or merge into one-piece topology.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- wall-assisted contrapposto with near hip toward lens, far leg long, fingertips touching neck line.
- close-range pose lock: one weight-bearing leg plus one display leg, visible S-curve through ankle-hip-sternum, active fingers/jawline/core tension, direct-lens intimacy without explicit content.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- wall reaction -> clavicle lift -> ribcage counter-rotation -> seam stress migration -> slit angle shift -> toe pressure recovery.
- Anatomy guardrail: human-plausible joint ranges only; clear load path from support to pelvis to ribcage to gaze; no hyperextension or disconnected limb angles.

CAMERA + LIGHTING PROFILE:
- Leica Q3 43, 43mm, f/2.0, 1/160s, ISO 1400, warm practicals + focused spot spill.

COMPOSITION REQUIREMENTS:
- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.

2) Wardrobe fidelity: exact garment topology, colors, seam map, and material behavior.
3) Pose mechanics: human-plausible balance, support loads, and coherent contact points.
4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- midnight atrium portrait with chandelier glow and intimate tension.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- hanging crystal fixtures, black stone floor reflections, brass columns, low haze.
- intimate environment lock: private-hour nightlife mood, low-key practicals with warm/cool contrast, no sterile daytime or generic lobby atmosphere.

WARDROBE LOCK (EXACT):
- ice-gold satin one-shoulder crop with side aperture + deep-emerald contour-slit skirt with bias fold, black thigh-high stockings, silver pumps.
- Styling edge lock: preserve assertive cut lines and fabric tension (slit/mesh/cutout intent); never conservative-restyle or merge into one-piece topology.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- long-stride freeze with pelvis leading and shoulder opposition, clutch hand weighted realistically.
- close-range pose lock: one weight-bearing leg plus one display leg, visible S-curve through ankle-hip-sternum, active fingers/jawline/core tension, direct-lens intimacy without explicit content.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- forward momentum -> shoulder counter-rotation -> skirt drag vector -> clutch inertia -> forefoot load -> COM capture.
- Anatomy guardrail: human-plausible joint ranges only; clear load path from support to pelvis to ribcage to gaze; no hyperextension or disconnected limb angles.

CAMERA + LIGHTING PROFILE:
- Leica SL3, 45mm, f/2.2, 1/160s, ISO 1200, warm chandelier key + cool fill.

COMPOSITION REQUIREMENTS:
- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.

3) Pose mechanics: human-plausible balance, support loads, and coherent contact points.
4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- bedside lamp edge lean with intentional nightlife atmosphere and strong physical plausibility.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- Private suite bedside lounge, one warm lamp, city lights diffused through sheer drape.
- Intimate luxury-suite mood only; no public venue cues.

WARDROBE LOCK (EXACT):
- assertive two-piece editorial attire only (not evening wear; no one-piece fallback): deep-plum lace balconette crop with micro-boned side panels + asymmetric pencil skirt with satin underlayer and angled slit.
- Black sheer thigh-high hosiery with visible denier gradient and pressure-consistent top band.
- High-gloss pointed stilettos in dark cherry lacquer.
- Waist separation must remain unmistakable, camera-legible, and non-explicit.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- Balanced full-body stance with direct eye contact, active hands, and clear load path.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- Support reaction -> pelvic orientation -> ribcage counter-rotation -> limb tension -> grounded foot mechanics.

CAMERA + LIGHTING PROFILE:
- Canon R5 II, 45mm, f/1.8, 1/200s, ISO 1250.

COMPOSITION REQUIREMENTS:
- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.

4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.

- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

## Prompt 89 - Dining Banquette Candle Reach

### Primary Prompt

Create a premium non-explicit nightlife editorial frame with exact identity fidelity, strong physics realism, and consistent microdetail.

3) Pose mechanics: human-plausible balance, support loads, and coherent contact points.
4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

- Support reaction -> pelvic orientation -> ribcage counter-rotation -> limb tension -> grounded foot mechanics.

CAMERA + LIGHTING PROFILE:
- Leica SL2-S, 50mm, f/2.0, 1/160s, ISO 1200.

COMPOSITION REQUIREMENTS:
- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.

## Prompt 94 - Coffee Table Forward-Lunge Hold

### Primary Prompt

MISSION:
Create a premium non-explicit nightlife editorial frame with exact identity fidelity, strong physics realism, and consistent microdetail.

GOAL ORDER (HARD):
1) Identity fidelity + direct lens eye contact.
2) Wardrobe fidelity: exact garment topology, colors, seam map, and material behavior.
3) Pose mechanics: human-plausible balance, support loads, and coherent contact points.
4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- coffee table forward-lunge hold with intentional nightlife atmosphere and strong physical plausibility.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- Intimate suite salon with low coffee table, velvet sofa, art books, and practical lamp pools.
- Hero props and surfaces that must remain visible: coffee-table edge, art-book stack, velvet sofa seam line.
- Keep this frame unmistakably private, intimate, and premium luxury-suite only.

- 1) rose-black lace crop with satin seam tracing and reinforced under-bust channel
- 2) black lace high-slit skirt with crossover panel and satin inner facing

- Pointed high-gloss stilettos with coherent heel-floor load transfer.
- Clear top/skirt waist separation is mandatory.
- Hard topology rule: detached top and detached skirt remain separate garments; never merge into one-piece dress.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- Balanced full-body stance with direct eye contact, active hands, and clear load path.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- Support reaction -> pelvic orientation -> ribcage counter-rotation -> limb tension -> grounded foot mechanics.

- Full body visible; clear foreground-midground-background separation.
- Strong leading lines toward eyes and face.
- Natural limb spacing, no fused geometry, no mannequin stillness.
- Keep one coherent lens profile and one coherent lighting strategy.

HARD REJECT:
- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe topology drift, impossible joints.
- Flat lighting, detached shadows/reflections, plastic skin, geometry collapse.
- Conservative restyle, all-black substitution collapse, one-piece fusion errors.
- Any explicit or disallowed framing.


### Safe Backup Prompt

MISSION:

MANDATORY LOCKS:

- 1) emerald-black lace crop with satin contour piping and reinforced under-bust frame
- 2) black lace slit skirt with asymmetric overlap and structured side panel
- Black thigh-high hosiery with visible denier gradient, upper-band compression transition, and angle-dependent sheen.
- Pointed high-gloss stilettos with coherent heel-floor load transfer.
- Clear top/skirt waist separation is mandatory.
- Hard topology rule: detached top and detached skirt remain separate garments; never merge into one-piece dress.

- Balanced full-body pose with direct gaze and coherent support mechanics.
- Support reaction -> pelvic orientation -> ribcage counter-rotation -> limb tension -> grounded foot mechanics.

- Contact compression + contact shadows at heels/seat/hand interfaces.

- Identity drift, off-camera gaze, wardrobe drift, geometry fusion.

## Prompt 99 - Velvet Ottoman Elevated-Leg Pause

### Primary Prompt

MISSION:
Create a premium non-explicit nightlife editorial frame with exact identity fidelity, strong physics realism, and consistent microdetail.

GOAL ORDER (HARD):
1) Identity fidelity + direct lens eye contact.
2) Wardrobe fidelity: exact garment topology, colors, seam map, and material behavior.
3) Pose mechanics: human-plausible balance, support loads, and coherent contact points.
4) Scene credibility: practical-light behavior, depth layering, and surface interaction.
5) Microdetail integrity: skin texture, fabric dynamics, reflection correctness, sensor realism.

NON-EXPLICIT LIMITS (MANDATORY):
- Adult subject only.
- Non-explicit framing only.
- No nudity and no explicit sexual context.

PHYSICS CHECKLIST (ALL MUST PASS):
- Inverse-square practical-light falloff with believable near/far contrast.
- Contact compression and contact shadow coherence at every support interface.
- Stable center-of-mass projection inside support base; no floating load paths.
- Cloth anisotropy and wrinkle hierarchy (macro drape, meso seam buckling, micro strain creases).
- Slit/hem/mesh response follows pose chain and gravity direction.
- Hosiery denier/translucency gradients and cuff-pressure transitions remain coherent.
- Material optics stay distinct: skin soft rolloff, metal tight highlights, satin directional sheen.
- Reflection integrity: no detached reflections, roughness-governed blur/intensity.
- Camera realism: natural grain, no plastic smoothing, plausible depth-of-field transition.

CRITICAL ZONE CHECKLIST (MANDATORY):
- heel-floor contact: compression, shadow anchoring, and toe-roll plausibility.
- thigh-band transition: pressure gradient, translucency change, and skin/fabric boundary continuity.
- slit-boundary mechanics: seam tension, edge curvature, and gravity-aligned opening behavior.
- knee contour + ankle instep: tendon/skin strain alignment with support force.
- hand-support interface: knuckle pressure, tendon engagement, and micro-shadow adhesion.
- jawline/eye-line lock: direct gaze, facial asymmetry realism, and expression control.

SCENE INTENT:
- velvet ottoman elevated-leg pause with intentional nightlife atmosphere and strong physical plausibility.

SCENE ANCHORS (LOCK):
- Intimate luxury suite lounge with jewel-tone velvet ottoman, brass floor lamp, and dark wood backdrop.

- Keep this frame unmistakably private, intimate, and premium luxury-suite only.

- 1) sapphire lace crop with satin panel understructure and delicate lace strapwork
- 2) black-sapphire lace slit skirt with sculpted side darts and satin lining
- Black thigh-high hosiery with visible denier gradient, upper-band compression transition, and angle-dependent sheen.
- Pointed high-gloss stilettos with coherent heel-floor load transfer.
- Clear top/skirt waist separation is mandatory.
- Hard topology rule: detached top and detached skirt remain separate garments; never merge into one-piece dress.

POSE BLUEPRINT (EXACT):
- Balanced full-body stance with direct eye contact, active hands, and clear load path.

KINEMATIC PATH (LOCK):
- Support reaction -> pelvic orientation -> ribcage counter-rotation -> limb tension -> grounded foot mechanics.
